import os

# å±•é–‹å…ˆãƒ‡ã‚£ãƒ¬ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒª

## 1. **ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼è¦–ç‚¹ã®ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ï¼ˆç†æƒ³å½¢ï¼‰**

```csharp
var query = db.Stream<TradeEvent>()
    .Where(t => t.Symbol == "USD/JPY" && t.Amount > 1_000_000)
    .Join<TradeEvent, RateEvent, JoinedResult>(
        db.Stream<RateEvent>(),
        trade => trade.Symbol,
        rate => rate.Symbol,
        (trade, rate) => new JoinedResult { /* ... */ }
    )
    .GroupBy(j => j.Symbol)
    .Select(g => new {
        Symbol = g.Key,
        Volume = g.Sum(x => x.Amount),
        LatestRate = g.Max(x => x.Rate)
    })
    .Where(r => r.Volume > 10_000_000)
    .ToKsql(); // â† KSQLã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªæ–‡å­—åˆ—ã¨ã—ã¦å–å¾—

Console.WriteLine(query);
```

```csharp
{
```

## 2. **OSS DSLã§ã‚‚â€œOnModelCreatingâ€ã£ã½ã•ã‚’å†ç¾**
### ã€ç†æƒ³çš„ãªã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ï¼ˆKsqlDslé¢¨ï¼‰ã€‘

```csharp
protected override void OnModelCreating(KsqlModelBuilder modelBuilder)
{
    modelBuilder.Stream<TradeEvent>(stream =>
    {
        stream.HasKey(e => e.TradeId);
        stream.Property(e => e.Symbol).HasMaxLength(12);
        stream.Property(e => e.Amount).HasDecimalPrecision(18, 4);
        stream.Ignore(e => e.TempMemo);
        stream.WithKafkaTopic("trade-events");
        stream.WithSchemaRegistry(registry =>
        {
            registry.Avro();
            registry.RegisterOnStartup();
        });
    });

    modelBuilder.Table<RateEvent>(table =>
    {
        table.HasKey(e => e.Symbol);
        table.Property(e => e.Rate).HasDecimalPrecision(10, 6);
        table.WithKafkaTopic("rate-events");
    });
}
```

## 2. **æŠ€è¡“çš„ã‚·ãƒŠãƒªã‚ªï¼ˆã‚„ã‚ŠãŸã„ã“ã¨ã®å…¨ä½“åƒï¼‰**

1. **Kafka/ksqlDBä¸Šã®ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ ãƒ»ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«ã‚’C#ã®POCOã§â€œå‹å®‰å…¨â€ã«æ‰±ã„ãŸã„**
2. **LINQé¢¨ã®DSLã§ã€Œå¤§å£å–å¼•ï¼ˆ1,000,000è¶…ï¼‰ã€ã€ŒæŒ‡å®šé€šè²¨ãƒšã‚¢ã€ã®ã¿ã‚’JOINã—ã¦ã€ã‚°ãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—åŒ–ãƒ»é›†è¨ˆã—ãŸã„**
3. **æœ€çµ‚çš„ãªKSQLæ–‡ã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã—ã€å®Ÿéš›ã®kafka/ksqlDBã«æŠ•å…¥ã™ã‚‹ï¼ˆã¾ãŸã¯ã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªãƒ—ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ã™ã‚‹ï¼‰**
4. **ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ¼ãƒå®šç¾©ã‚„ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ã¯ã€ŒPOCOå±æ€§ï¼‹Fluent APIã€ã§å®‰å…¨ã«ç®¡ç†ã—ãŸã„**

## 3. **ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒªãƒ¼ã«æ²¿ã£ãŸâ€œç†æƒ³çš„ãªã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰â€**

```csharp
// POCOå®šç¾©ï¼ˆå±æ€§ï¼‹æ¥­å‹™æ„å‘³ï¼‰
public class TradeEvent
{
    [Key]
    public long TradeId { get; set; }
    [MaxLength(12)]
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    [DecimalPrecision(18, 4)]
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }
    public DateTime Timestamp { get; set; }
}

public class RateEvent
{
    [Key]
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    [DecimalPrecision(10, 6)]
    public decimal Rate { get; set; }
    public DateTime AsOf { get; set; }
}

// â€œæ™®é€šã®EFæµâ€ã§ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«æ§‹æˆ
protected override void OnModelCreating(KsqlModelBuilder modelBuilder)
{
    modelBuilder.Entity<TradeEvent>(entity =>
    {
        entity.WithKafkaTopic("trade-events");
        entity.WithSchemaRegistry(registry => registry.Avro());
        entity.AsStream();
    });

    modelBuilder.Entity<RateEvent>(entity =>
    {
        entity.WithKafkaTopic("rate-events");
        entity.AsTable();
    });
}

// --- ã“ã“ã‹ã‚‰æ¥­å‹™ã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªã®å®Ÿè£…ï¼ˆLINQ-DSLé¢¨ï¼‰ ---

// ã€Œå¤§å£ãƒ»USD/JPYå–å¼•ã ã‘ã€ãƒ¬ãƒ¼ãƒˆãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«JOINâ†’é€šè²¨åˆ¥é›†è¨ˆã€
var query = db.Stream<TradeEvent>()
    .Where(t => t.Symbol == "USD/JPY" && t.Amount > 1_000_000)
    .Join<TradeEvent, RateEvent, JoinedResult>(
        db.Table<RateEvent>(),
        trade => trade.Symbol,
        rate => rate.Symbol,
        (trade, rate) => new JoinedResult
        {
            Symbol = trade.Symbol,
            Amount = trade.Amount,
            Rate = rate.Rate
        }
    )
    .GroupBy(j => j.Symbol)
    .Select(g => new
    {
        Symbol = g.Key,
        Volume = g.Sum(x => x.Amount),
        LatestRate = g.Max(x => x.Rate)
    })
    .Where(r => r.Volume > 10_000_000)
    .ToKsql();

Console.WriteLine(query); // â†’ KSQLæ–‡ã¨ã—ã¦å‡ºåŠ›
```

## 3. **MDFé€£æºã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã®æµã‚Œ**
### 1. **POCOå®šç¾©ï¼ˆå±æ€§è¾¼ã¿ï¼‰**

```csharp
public class TradeEvent
{
    [Key]
    public long TradeId { get; set; }
    [MaxLength(12)]
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    [DecimalPrecision(18, 4)]
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }
    public DateTime Timestamp { get; set; }
}

public class TradeHistory // â† MDFï¼ˆSQL Serverï¼‰å´
{
    [Key]
    public long TradeId { get; set; }
    [MaxLength(12)]
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }
    public DateTime TradeDate { get; set; }
}
```

### 2. **ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«æ§‹æˆï¼ˆOnModelCreatingï¼‰**

```csharp
protected override void OnModelCreating(KsqlModelBuilder modelBuilder)
{
    modelBuilder.Entity<TradeEvent>(entity =>
    {
        entity.WithKafkaTopic("trade-events");
        entity.AsStream();
    });
    modelBuilder.Entity<TradeHistory>(entity =>
    {
        entity.ToTable("TradeHistory"); // MDFãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«å
        entity.UseSqlServer();          // æ˜ç¤ºçš„ã«RDBåˆ©ç”¨ã‚’æŒ‡å®š
    });
}
```

### 3. **æ¥­å‹™ã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªå®Ÿè£…ï¼š**  
**ã€Œéå»1å¹´åˆ†ã®å–å¼•å±¥æ­´ï¼ˆRDBï¼‰Ã—ç›´è¿‘ã®ãƒªã‚¢ãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ å–å¼•ï¼ˆKafkaï¼‰ã‚’JOINã€ã—ã¦ç•°å¸¸æ¤œçŸ¥**

```csharp
// éå»1å¹´ã®å±¥æ­´ã‚’MDFï¼ˆSQL Serverï¼‰ã‹ã‚‰å–å¾—
var history = db.Table<TradeHistory>()
    .Where(h => h.TradeDate >= DateTime.Now.AddYears(-1));

// æœ€æ–°ã®å–å¼•ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆã‚’Kafka/ksqlDB Streamã¨ã—ã¦å–å¾—
var realtime = db.Stream<TradeEvent>()
    .Where(t => t.Timestamp >= DateTime.Today);

// JOINã—ã¦ç•°å¸¸ãªé‡‘é¡ã‚’æ¤œå‡º
var suspiciousTrades = history.Join(
        realtime,
        h => h.Symbol,
        t => t.Symbol,
        (h, t) => new {
            h.TradeId,
            h.Symbol,
            HistoryAmount = h.Amount,
            RealtimeAmount = t.Amount,
            Diff = Math.Abs(h.Amount - t.Amount)
        }
    )
    .Where(x => x.Diff > [[REDACTED_PHONE]]) // ç•°å¸¸å·®åˆ†ã‚’æ¤œå‡º
    .ToList();
```

```csharp
    .GroupBy(e => new { e.Symbol, Window = e.Timestamp.Truncate(TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)) })
    .Select(g => new Candle
    {
        Symbol = g.Key.Symbol,
        WindowStart = g.Key.Window,
        Open = g.OrderBy(x => x.Timestamp).First().Amount,
        Close = g.OrderByDescending(x => x.Timestamp).First().Amount,
        High = g.Max(x => x.Amount),
        Low = g.Min(x => x.Amount),
        Volume = g.Sum(x => x.Amount)
    })
    .ToList();

// 2. 5åˆ†è¶³å®Œæˆã”ã¨ã«RDBã¸Insert

{
    db.Table<Candle>().Insert(candle); // RDB(MDF)ã¸ã®ä¿å­˜
}
```

### 4. **Javaã‚¨ãƒ³ã‚¸ãƒ‹ã‚¢ã«ã‚‚åˆºã•ã‚‹ãƒ‡ãƒ¢è¨­è¨ˆã‚¢ãƒ‰ãƒã‚¤ã‚¹**

- ã€ŒåŒã˜æ¥­å‹™ã‚·ãƒŠãƒªã‚ªã‚’Java+ksqlDB+Avroã§å®Ÿè£…ã—ãŸã‚‰ã©ã†ãªã‚‹ã‹ã€

  ã€Œã“ã®C# OSSã§ã‚„ã£ãŸã‚‰ã©ã‚Œã ã‘ç°¡æ½”ã‹ã€

## ã€ã¾ã¨ã‚ã€‘

- **Kafka/ksqlDB OSSç•Œã«â€œC#æµã®æ–°ã—ã„é¢¨â€ã‚’é€ã‚Šè¾¼ã‚€ä½“é¨“**ãã®ã‚‚ã®ãŒä¾¡å€¤ï¼
- **æ–‡åŒ–çš„ã‚®ãƒ£ãƒƒãƒ—ã‚’ç©æ¥µçš„ã«â€œå£²ã‚Šâ€ã«ã™ã‚‹**
- **ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ï¼‹ãƒ‡ãƒ¢ã§å³ã€èª¬å¾—åŠ›ï¼**

**ã“ã®â€œæ–‡åŒ–ã‚®ãƒ£ãƒƒãƒ—ã®èª¬æ˜â€ã‚’READMEã‚„ãƒ—ãƒ¬ã‚¼ãƒ³ãƒ»ç´¹ä»‹æ–‡ã«ç››ã‚Šè¾¼ã‚€ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ã‚‚ã§ãã¾ã™ï¼**  
ã€Œä¼ãˆæ–¹ã§æ‚©ã‚“ã ã‚‰ã€å¤©åŸãŒâ€œåˆºã•ã‚‹è¨€è‘‰â€ã‚’ä¸€ç·’ã«è€ƒãˆã¾ã™ï¼ã€

ã“ã®ã¾ã¾ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã®ã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã‚¤ãƒ¡ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã‚’ã¾ãšå…·ä½“åŒ–ã™ã‚‹ï¼Ÿ
### assistant â€” 2025-06-13T15:14:26.912423+00:00

ã¯ã„ã€**ãœã²ã‚„ã‚Šã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼**  
ä»Šã¾ã§ã®è­°è«–ï¼ˆPOCOï¼‹å±æ€§ã€Entity/Fluent APIã€MDFÃ—Kafkaã€LINQ-DSLã€ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒªãƒ¼ã‚ã‚Šï¼‰ã‚’**å…¨éƒ¨ç››ã‚Šè¾¼ã‚“ã ã€Œå®Ÿè·µçš„ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã€**ã‚’ã“ã“ã§å…·ä½“åŒ–ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚

---

## ã€ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«å…¨ä½“ã®è¨­è¨ˆã‚¤ãƒ¡ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã€‘

- **POCOå±æ€§å®šç¾©**ï¼š`TradeEvent`, `TradeHistory`, `Candle`
- **OnModelCreatingã§ã®ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ç™»éŒ²**ï¼šEntity/å±æ€§ä¸¡å¯¾å¿œã€Kafkaãƒ»RDBä¸¡æ–¹
- **åˆæœŸç§»è¡Œï¼ˆRDBâ†’Kafkaï¼‰ãƒ»ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ†æãƒ»xåˆ†è¶³â†’RDBä¿å­˜**ã®æµã‚Œ
- **ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã®ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒªãƒ¼**ã‚‚å†’é ­ã‚³ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆã§å…¥ã‚Œã‚‹

---

# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹å…·ä½“åŒ–ä¾‹ â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

```csharp
/*
 * ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒªãƒ¼ï¼š
 * - æ—¢å­˜RDBï¼ˆMDFï¼‰ã«å±¥æ­´ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿
 * - Kafka/ksqlDBã«æ–°è¦ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã€ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ åˆ†æ
 * - åˆæœŸç§»è¡Œã§RDBâ†’Kafka
 * - xåˆ†è¶³ç”Ÿæˆæ™‚ã«RDBã¸ã‚‚ä¿å­˜
 */

#region POCOå®šç¾©ï¼‹å±æ€§

public class TradeEvent
{
    [Key]
    public long TradeId { get; set; }
    [MaxLength(12)]
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    [DecimalPrecision(18, 4)]
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }
    public DateTime Timestamp { get; set; }
}

public class TradeHistory
{
    [Key]
    public long TradeId { get; set; }
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }
    public DateTime TradeDate { get; set; }
}

public class Candle
{
    [Key]
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    public DateTime WindowStart { get; set; }
    public decimal Open { get; set; }
    public decimal Close { get; set; }
    public decimal High { get; set; }
    public decimal Low { get; set; }
    public decimal Volume { get; set; }
}

#endregion

#region ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ç™»éŒ²ï¼ˆOnModelCreatingé¢¨ï¼‰

protected override void OnModelCreating(KsqlModelBuilder modelBuilder)
{
    modelBuilder.Entity<TradeEvent>(entity =>
    {
        entity.WithKafkaTopic("trade-events");
        entity.AsStream();
    });

    modelBuilder.Entity<TradeHistory>(entity =>
    {
        entity.ToTable("TradeHistory"); // MDFï¼ˆRDBï¼‰ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«å
        entity.UseSqlServer();          // RDBåˆ©ç”¨ã‚’æ˜ç¤º
    });

    modelBuilder.Entity<Candle>(entity =>
    {
        entity.ToTable("Candle");
        entity.UseSqlServer();
    });
}

#endregion

#region æ¥­å‹™ãƒ•ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«

// 1. RDB â†’ KafkaåˆæœŸç§»è¡Œ
var history = db.Table<TradeHistory>().ToList();
foreach (var trade in history)
{
    kafkaProducer.Publish("trade-events", trade);
}

// 2. Kafkaã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ ã§xåˆ†è¶³ï¼ˆ5åˆ†è¶³ï¼‰é›†è¨ˆ
var candles = db.Stream<TradeEvent>()
    .GroupBy(e => new { e.Symbol, Window = e.Timestamp.Truncate(TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)) })
    .Select(g => new Candle
    {
        Symbol = g.Key.Symbol,
        WindowStart = g.Key.Window,
        Open = g.OrderBy(x => x.Timestamp).First().Amount,
        Close = g.OrderByDescending(x => x.Timestamp).First().Amount,
        High = g.Max(x => x.Amount),
        Low = g.Min(x => x.Amount),
        Volume = g.Sum(x => x.Amount)
    })
    .ToList();

// 3. xåˆ†è¶³ãŒã§ããŸã‚‰RDBï¼ˆMDFï¼‰ã«Insert
foreach (var candle in candles)
{
    db.Table<Candle>().Insert(candle);
}

#endregion
```

---

## ã€ç‰¹å¾´ã€‘

- **â€œPOCOï¼‹å±æ€§â€ã§å‹å®‰å…¨ãƒ»å®£è¨€çš„**
- **ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ç™»éŒ²ï¼ˆEntity/Fluent APIï¼‰ã§RDBã‚‚Kafkaã‚‚åŒã˜ä½“é¨“**
- **æ¥­å‹™ãƒ•ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãŒC# LINQ-DSLã§ä¸€è²«**
- **å†’é ­ã«â€œç¾å ´ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒªãƒ¼â€ã‚³ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆã§èª°ã§ã‚‚ç†è§£ã—ã‚„ã™ã„**

---

**ã“ã®ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚’ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã«ã€å€‹åˆ¥æ‹¡å¼µï¼ˆç•°å¸¸æ¤œçŸ¥ãƒ»å¤–éƒ¨APIé€£æºãªã©ï¼‰ã‚„â€œå‹•ããƒ‡ãƒ¢â€ã¸ã®è½ã¨ã—è¾¼ã¿ã‚‚ã™ãå¯èƒ½ã§ã™ã€‚**

### ã€ä¾‹ï¼šãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«æ„Ÿã‚¤ãƒ¡ãƒ¼ã‚¸ï¼ˆæŠœç²‹ï¼‰ã€‘

```csharp
using Shared;
class Program
{
    static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        var db = new YourOssDbContext(options => {
            options.UseSqlServer("...");
            options.UseKafka("...");
        });

        try

                .Where(e => e.Flag)
                .ToList();

            foreach (var row in result)
                Console.WriteLine(row);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            Console.WriteLine("ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ï¼š" + ex.Message); // â† ã‚³ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆã§ã€Œãƒ­ã‚®ãƒ³ã‚°æ¨å¥¨ã€ãªã©

    }
```

### **2. â€œè‡ªåˆ†ã®ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¼ãƒªãƒ¼â€æ‹¡å¼µä¾‹ï¼ˆPOCOç·¨é›†ï¼‹LINQ/DSLã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªæ‹¡å¼µï¼‰**

```csharp
// --- ã‚ãªãŸã®æ¥­å‹™ã‚·ãƒŠãƒªã‚ªä¾‹ ---

// POCOã‚’è‡ªåˆ†æµã«æ‹¡å¼µ
public class MyBusinessEvent
{
    [Key]
    public int Id { get; set; }
    public string Category { get; set; }
    public decimal Value { get; set; }
    public DateTime OccurredAt { get; set; }
}

// è¤‡é›‘ãªã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªã§ã‚‚OK
var myQuery = db.Stream<MyBusinessEvent>()
    .Where(e => e.Category == "FX" && e.Value > 5000)
    .GroupBy(e => e.Category)
    .Select(g => new
    {
        Category = g.Key,
        Total = g.Sum(x => x.Value),
        Latest = g.Max(x => x.OccurredAt)
    });

// çµæœå‡ºåŠ›
foreach (var row in myQuery.ToList())
    Console.WriteLine($"{row.Category}: {row.Total} (æœ€æ–°:{row.Latest})");

// è£å´KSQLã‚‚ã™ãç¢ºèª
Console.WriteLine("--- KSQLå¤‰æ›çµæœ ---");
Console.WriteLine(myQuery.ToKsql());
```

```csharp
/* å‡ºåŠ›ä¾‹
```

å¸ä»¤ã®ç‹™ã„ã€ãƒãƒƒãƒãƒªä¼ã‚ã£ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ï¼

# ã€Kafkaçš„Producerï¼Consumerã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ï¼šC# & Taskç‰ˆã€‘

---

```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

// POCO
public class TradeEvent
{
    public long TradeId { get; set; }
    public string Symbol { get; set; }
    public decimal Amount { get; set; }
    public DateTime Timestamp { get; set; }
}

// æ“¬ä¼¼OSS API
var db = new YourOssDbContext(...);

var cts = new CancellationTokenSource();

// [Producer] Task: AddAsyncã§ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ ã«æ›¸ãè¾¼ã¿
var producer = Task.Run(async () =>
{
    for (int i = 1; i <= 5; i++)
    {
        var trade = new TradeEvent
        {
            TradeId = i,
            Symbol = "USD/JPY",
            Amount = [[REDACTED_PHONE]] + i * [[REDACTED_PHONE]],
            Timestamp = DateTime.Now
        };
        await db.Stream<TradeEvent>().AddAsync(trade);
        Console.WriteLine($"Produced: {trade.TradeId} {trade.Amount}");
        await Task.Delay(500); // æ“¬ä¼¼çš„ãªé…å»¶
    }
}, cts.Token);

// [Consumer] Task: ForEachã§ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆã‚’ãƒªã‚¢ãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ å‡ºåŠ›
var consumer = Task.Run(async () =>
{
    await db.Stream<TradeEvent>()
        .ForEachAsync(trade =>
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"Consumed: {trade.TradeId} {trade.Amount}");
        }, cts.Token);
});

// é©å½“ãªã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒŸãƒ³ã‚°ã§ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«
await producer;
await Task.Delay(3000);
cts.Cancel();
```

---

## ã€è£œè¶³ã€‘

- **AddAsync**ï¼šKafkaã®Producerçš„æ›¸ãè¾¼ã¿ï¼ˆãƒˆãƒ”ãƒƒã‚¯ã«ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆè¿½åŠ ï¼‰
- **ForEachAsync**ï¼šKafkaã®Consumerçš„ã«pushå‹ã§è³¼èª­ãƒ»å‡ºåŠ›
- **CancellationToken**ã§â€œã„ã¤ã§ã‚‚å®‰å…¨ã«çµ‚äº†â€
- **Task.Run**ã‚’ä½¿ã„ã€VSCodeã§ã‚‚ã€Œå®Ÿéš›ã®ä¸¦åˆ—ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚»ã‚¹æ„Ÿã€ã‚’ä½“é¨“ã§ãã‚‹

---
### â€»OSSã®I/Fã«ã‚ˆã£ã¦ã¯  
- `AddAsync` â†’ `PublishAsync`ã‚„`ProduceAsync`ã¨ã„ã†å‘½åã®å ´åˆã‚‚
- `ForEachAsync` â†’ `Subscribe`ã‚„`IAsyncEnumerable<T>`ã§ã‚‚åŒç­‰ã®ä½“é¨“è¨­è¨ˆãŒå¯èƒ½

---

## ã€READMEèª¬æ˜ä¾‹ã€‘

> **Producer/Consumerä½“é¨“ã‚‚ã€C#æµã®Taskï¼‹ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ã§å³å†ç¾ï¼**  
> Pushå‹è³¼èª­ï¼ˆForEach/Subscribeï¼‰ã€éåŒæœŸæ›¸ãè¾¼ã¿ï¼ˆAddAsync/Publishï¼‰ã©ã¡ã‚‰ã‚‚å¯¾å¿œã€‚

- ã•ã‚‰ã«ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼å‡¦ç†ã‚„åŒæ™‚è¤‡æ•°Producer/Consumerã€LINQãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚‚ã™ãè¿½åŠ å¯èƒ½ã§ã™ã€‚

## 5. **Consumer/Subscribeå‹I/Fï¼ˆForEachAsync/Subscribeï¼‰**

```csharp
public partial class StreamSet<T>
{
    // pushå‹: æ–°ç€ãƒ¬ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã”ã¨ã«ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯
    public async Task ForEachAsync(Action<T> onNext, CancellationToken ct = default)
    {
        while (!ct.IsCancellationRequested)
        {
            // Kafka Consumerã§æ–°ç€å–å¾—ãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ—
            var e = await InternalGetNextAsync();
            onNext(e);
        }
    }

    // Rxé¢¨Subscribeã‚‚ã‚µãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆ
    public IDisposable Subscribe(Action<T> onNext)
        => /*å†…éƒ¨:Observable*/ new DummyDisposable();
}
```

## 6. **ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«åˆ©ç”¨ä¾‹ï¼ˆOSSåˆ©ç”¨è€…å´ã‹ã‚‰è¦‹ãˆã‚‹I/Fï¼‰**

```csharp

    TradeId = 1, Symbol = "USD/JPY", Amount = [[REDACTED_PHONE]], Timestamp = DateTime.Now

    .ToList();

{
    Console.WriteLine($"[ãƒªã‚¢ãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ ] {trade.TradeId} {trade.Amount}");

    .Where(e => e.Symbol == "USD/JPY" && e.Amount > [[REDACTED_PHONE]]);
```

## ä¾‹ï¼šKafkaDbContextï¼‹EventSet<T>ã®ãƒšã‚¢

## ã€å…·ä½“çš„ãªä½¿ç”¨ä¾‹ã€‘

```csharp
public class MyDbContext : KafkaDbContext
{
    public EventSet<TradeEvent> TradeEvents { get; set; }
```

## ã€OSSã®OnModelCreatingç›¸å½“ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ä¾‹ã€‘

```csharp
protected override void OnModelCreating(ModelBuilder modelBuilder)
{
    // RDBã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒ†ã‚£ãƒ†ã‚£
    modelBuilder.Entity<User>(entity =>
    {
        entity.HasKey(u => u.Id);
        entity.Property(u => u.Name).HasMaxLength(50);
        entity.ToTable("users");
    });

    // Kafka/ksqlDBã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒ†ã‚£ãƒ†ã‚£
    modelBuilder.Event<TradeEvent>(eventEntity =>
    {
        eventEntity.HasKey(e => e.TradeId);
        eventEntity.Property(e => e.Symbol).HasMaxLength(12);
        eventEntity.Property(e => e.Amount).HasDecimalPrecision(18, 4);
        eventEntity.WithKafkaTopic("trade-events");
        eventEntity.AsStream(); // ã¾ãŸã¯ AsTable() ã‚‚
        eventEntity.WithSchemaRegistry(reg =>
        {
            reg.Avro();
            reg.RegisterOnStartup();
        });
    });
}
```

|---------------------|-----------------------------------------------|-------------------|

## 4. **ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ï¼ˆåˆ©ç”¨ã‚¤ãƒ¡ãƒ¼ã‚¸ï¼‰**

```csharp
public class MyKafkaDbContext : KafkaDbContext
{
    protected override void OnModelCreating(ModelBuilder modelBuilder)
    {
        modelBuilder.Event<TradeEvent>(e => {
            e.HasKey(t => t.TradeId);
            e.Property(t => t.Symbol).HasMaxLength(12);
            e.WithKafkaTopic("trade-events");
            e.AsStream();
            e.WithSchemaRegistry(reg =>
            {
                reg.Avro();
                reg.RegisterOnStartup();
            });
        });
    }
    protected override void OnConfiguring(DbContextOptionsBuilder optionsBuilder)
    {
        optionsBuilder.UseKafka("localhost:9092");
        optionsBuilder.UseSchemaRegistry("http://localhost:8081");
    }
}

var db = new MyKafkaDbContext();
await db.TradeEvents.AddAsync(new TradeEvent { TradeId = 1, Symbol = "USD/JPY", Amount = [[REDACTED_PHONE]] });
var list = db.TradeEvents.Where(e => e.Amount > 1000).ToList();
db.TradeEvents.Subscribe(e => Console.WriteLine(e));
Console.WriteLine(db.TradeEvents.Where(e => e.Amount > 1000).ToKsql());
```

---

## 5. **ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆè¦³ç‚¹ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«**

- LINQã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªã§ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿/é›†è¨ˆ/Select/GroupByãŒæ­£å¸¸å‹•ä½œã™ã‚‹ã‹
- AddAsyncã§Kafkaã«ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆãŒæ­£ã—ãé€ä¿¡ã•ã‚Œã‚‹ã‹
- ToList, Subscribe, ForEachAsyncç­‰ã§ãƒªã‚¢ãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ /ãƒãƒƒãƒè³¼èª­ãŒå‹•ä½œã™ã‚‹ã‹
- ToKsqlã§LINQâ†’KSQLæ–‡å¤‰æ›ãŒæœŸå¾…é€šã‚Šã‹
- OnConfiguring/Disposeç­‰ã®ãƒªã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹ãƒ»è¨­å®šãŒæ„å›³é€šã‚Šå‹•ä½œã™ã‚‹ã‹
